kodeqsiT ar aris mowesrigebuli SromiTi movaleobis Sesrulebisas

daavadebiT an janmTelobisaTvis vnebis miyenebis Sedegad zianis


anazRaurebis samarTlebriv safuZvlebs awesrigebs saqarTvelos


prezidentis 1999 wlis 9 Tebervlis

1981 wlis 19 seqtembers i. a-Svilma miiRo sawarmoo travma, romlis


Sedegadac dakarga Sromis unari da daeniSna pensia. pensias Rebulobda


1982 wlis 24 noembridan 1994 wlis 1 oqtombramde.


pensiis odenoba ganisazRvra saSualo Tviuri anazRaurebisa da


yovelTviurad samedicino komisiis mier dadgenili Sromis unaris


daqveiTebis procentiT.

SeCerebasTan dakavSirebiT.


1995 wlidan organizaciam muSaoba ganaaxla, magram pensiis gacema


ar gaugrZelebia.

fuZvelze Sromisunarianobis dakargva ganisazRvra 60%-iT.

saxiT 197 larisa da 62 TeTris gadaxdis Sesaxeb; garda amisa, man moiTxo-


1351


va gasuli wlebis pensiis, sul 5103 larisa da 54 TeTris gadaxda, razec


Sps `mxatvarma~ uari ganacxada, ris gamoc mosarCelem mimarTa sasamarT-


los sarCeliT mopasuxeze zemoaRniSnuli Tanxebis dakisrebis Sesaxeb.


Tbilisis samgoris raionis sasamarTlos 1998 wlis 13 maisis


gadawyvetilebiT sarCeli dakmayofilda, magram Tbilisis saqalaqo


sasamarTlos Tavmjdomaris protestis safuZvelze amave sasamarTlos


prezidiumis 1999 wlis 15 martis dadgenilebiT sasamarTlos

pirveli instanciis sasamarTloSi.

odenoba da moiTxova Sps `mxatvarisaTvis~ wina wlebis pensiis 8605


larisa da yovelTviurad 155 laris gadaxdis dakisreba, rasac sa-


fuZvlad daudo Semdegi:


1994 wlis 1 oqtombramde igi iRebda 167 maneTs, rac dRevandeli


kursiT Seadgens 65 lars; im droisaTvis mas Sromis unari dakarguli


hqonda 25%-iT, e.i. 1994 wlis 1 oqtombridan 1996 wlis 1 martamde (17


Tveze) mas ekuTvnis 1105 lari (65 lari gamravlebuli 17 Tveze).


1996 wlis martidan dekembramde, anu 10 Tvis manZilze mas Sromis


dakargvis procenti ganesazRvra 50%-iT, am periodSi ekuTvnis 1300


lari (130 lari gamravlebuli 10 Tveze).


1997 wlis ianvridan Sromis unaris daqveiTeba gansazRvrulia 60%-


iT, Sesabamisad, Tviuri pensia Seadgens 155 lars, xolo sarCelis Seta-


nis dRemde, 2000 wlis 1 maisamde, gadasaxdelia 40 Tvis pensia, rac Sead-


gens 6200 lars (155 lari gamravlebuli 40 Tveze).


sul gasuli wlebis pensiis Tanxa mosarCelis gaangariSebiT Sead-


gens 8605 lars (1105+1300+6200), xolo yovelTviurad mas unda daeniS-


nos 155 laris sarCo.

kombinatis teritoriis farglebs gareT. amasTan, ubeduri SemTxvevis


Sesaxeb Sedgenili aqti eWvs iwvevs, radgan masSi miTiTebuli pirovneba


1981 wels ar muSaobda kombinatSi; garda amisa, kombinats brali ar mi-


uZRvis momxdarSi, rac gamoricxavs mis pasuxismgeblobas.

tos gadawyvetilebiT i. a-Svils uari eTqva sarCelis dakmayofilebaze


usafuZvlobis gamo.


aRniSnuli gadawyvetileba gaasaCivra i. a-Svilma saapelacio wesiT.


man moiTxova saqmeze miRebuli gadawyvetilebis gauqmeba da misi


sarCelis dakmayofileba. apelantma damatebiT ganmarta, rom wlebis


manZilze kombinati uxdida mas pensias dasaxiCrebisaTvis da arasodes

kicebulebad, rom kombinatma aRiara Tavisi brali ubedur SemTxvevaSi

da ikisra valdebuleba muSakisaTvis miyenebuli zianis anazRaurebaze.

orjer ar gamocxadnen sazogadoebis krebaze, amasTan, daarRvies wesde-


bac, rac SeTqmulebis da Ralatis tolfasia. amiT isini gaemijnen sazo-

hqonia, ris gamoc ver uxdida mosarCeles dividendebs. mopasuxis
